+++

Caps annual rent increases for residential tenancies.

[Original Bill Text](https://olis.oregonlegislature.gov/liz/2023R1/Measures/Overview/SB611)

## Sponsors

**Chief Sponsors:** Wlnsvey Campos, Andrea Valderrama, Courtney Neron Misslin, Sara Gelser Blouin, Mark Gamba

**Co-Sponsors:** Michael Dembrow, Farrah Chaichi, Zach Hudson, Susan McLain, Khanh Pham, Aaron Woods


## Overview

<i>Limits</i>]<b> Caps</b> annual rent increases for residential tenancies. 
Declares emergency, effective on passage.
